  326 | async function withSupabaseTimeout(request, label = 'Supabase request', ms = 15000) {
  327 |   let timeoutId;
  328 | 
  329 |   const timeout = new Promise((_, reject) => {
  330 |     timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
  331 |       reject(new Error(label + ' timed out after ' + Math.round(ms / 1000) + ' seconds'));
  332 |     }, ms);
  333 |   });
  334 | 
  335 |   try {
  336 |     return await Promise.race([request, timeout]);
  337 |   } finally {
  338 |     clearTimeout(timeoutId);

 9174 |     body: JSON.stringify(patch)

 9168 | async function updateReferralDirect(id, patch) {
 9169 |   const url = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_URL;
 9170 | 
 9171 |   const response = await fetch(`${url}/rest/v1/referrals?id=eq.${encodeURIComponent(id)}&select=*`, {
 9172 |     method: "PATCH",
 9173 |     headers: await getSupabaseAuthHeaders(),
 9174 |     body: JSON.stringify(patch)
 9175 |   });
 9176 |
